3a:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":"Those fields are required, and that is the point. 41:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":"Every choice above holds up only if the graph is trustworthy, and that trust has to come from a real compiler."}]
42:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["A parser that only reads text, such as tree-sitter, stops where the syntax stops. It cannot follow a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"tsconfig"}]," ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"paths"}]," alias like ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@app/*"}]," to the real file, a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"workspace:*"}]," dependency into a sibling package, a symlink, or a re-export chain through a barrel ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"index.ts"}],". A compiler that has finished module resolution wires all of those up, and a guessed edge is exactly where an agent stops trusting the result and falls back to reading files."]}]
43:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@ttsc/graph"}]," reads the program ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"ttsc"}]," already type-checked, so its edges are resolved rather than inferred. The native compiler Program stays resident. Before each graph operation the server hashes the config chain, checks every root set and module-resolution input, and compares the current bytes of every Program source. With no change it returns the existing in-memory indexes. A content-only edit goes through tsgo’s incremental ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"UpdateProgram"}],"; an import-shape, config, addition, deletion, project-reference, or resolution change takes the safe full-reload path. A broken config fails the call instead of returning the previous graph."]}]
